CREATE CACHED TABLE PUBLIC.MY_USER(
    ID BIGINT DEFAULT (NEXT VALUE FOR PUBLIC.SYSTEM_SEQUENCE_64345E86_3981_4F74_B945_07094C4BAA59) NOT NULL NULL_TO_DEFAULT SEQUENCE PUBLIC.SYSTEM_SEQUENCE_64345E86_3981_4F74_B945_07094C4BAA59 SELECTIVITY 100,
    USERNAME VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL SELECTIVITY 100,
    NAME VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL SELECTIVITY 96,
    SURNAME VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL SELECTIVITY 99,
    DOCUMENT_TYPE VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL SELECTIVITY 1,
    DOCUMENT_NR VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL SELECTIVITY 100,
    EMAIL VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL SELECTIVITY 100,
    BIRTHDATE DATE NOT NULL SELECTIVITY 99,
    PESEL VARCHAR(11) NOT NULL SELECTIVITY 100,
    ELECTORAL_DISTRICT_ID BIGINT SELECTIVITY 9,
    MUNICIPALITY_ID BIGINT SELECTIVITY 3,
    ROLE VARCHAR2(255) SELECTIVITY 1
);
